# Top 50 Explosiveness Exercise Cards

Source basis: exercise_card_details_for_llm.md was used for Card v2 structure, canonical phase logic, Output placement, taxonomy tags, publish gates, and anti-patterns. Purpose.txt was requested but not found in the accessible File Library search results; this set uses the available authoring guide plus the user-provided explosiveness purpose.

## Top 50 by Category

### Acceleration / First-Step / Line-Off Explosiveness

| # | Exercise | Subrole | Equipment | Why it belongs |
|---:|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | Falling Start Sprint | Acceleration Start Speed | none, cones | Directly transfers to track starts, linemen firing off the line, and any athlete who must convert lean into projection. |
| 2 | 2-Point Acceleration Start | Acceleration Start Speed | cones | A clean general-purpose first-step drill for field, court, and track athletes without needing blocks. |
| 3 | Half-Kneeling Sprint Start | Acceleration Start Speed | cones | Useful when athletes need to explode from the ground or from a compromised stance while keeping trunk stiffness. |
| 4 | Push-Up Start Sprint | Acceleration Start Speed | none, cones | Links a fast push from the floor to sprint acceleration, valuable for football, wrestling, baseball, and chaotic field sport starts. |
| 5 | Prone Pop-Up to Sprint | Acceleration Start Speed | none, cones | Develops explosive transition from ground contact to acceleration without turning it into conditioning burpees. |
| 6 | Wall-Drive Switch to Sprint | Acceleration Start Speed | wall, cones | Bridges wall-drive mechanics to live sprinting and helps athletes feel shin angle, knee punch, and hip extension. |
| 7 | Light Sled Sprint Push | Acceleration Start Speed | sled, cones | Gives linemen and sprinters a forceful projection drill without making the sled a slow strength grind. |
| 8 | Partner Chase First-Step Sprint | Reactive Agility / Tumbling Output | partner, cones | Adds intent and reaction while preserving the training goal: win the first step, not survive repeated conditioning reps. |

### Elastic Foot-Ankle / Plyometric Rudiments

| # | Exercise | Subrole | Equipment | Why it belongs |
|---:|---|---|---|---|
| 9 | Pogo Jumps | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | none | Builds the foot-ankle stiffness needed for sprinting, jumping, and quick reactivity without heavy loading. |
| 10 | Line Hops | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | none, cones | Simple, scalable elastic work that trains short ground contact and foot speed in multiple directions. |
| 11 | Jump Rope Power Singles | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | jump_rope | Improves lower-leg elasticity, rhythm, and posture with easy dosage control and low space needs. |
| 12 | Single-Leg Pogo Jumps | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | none | Targets the single-leg elastic demand most athletes need when accelerating, jumping, cutting, and reacting. |
| 13 | A-Skip Rhythm Punch | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | none, cones | Connects stiffness to sprint rhythm without needing max velocity exposure or fatigue. |
| 14 | Pogo to 10-Yard Sprint | Acceleration Start Speed | cones | Teaches athletes to carry stiffness and posture from plyometric contacts into the first sprint steps. |
| 15 | Low Hurdle Quick Hop | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | cones | The barrier gives an external target while keeping height conservative enough to preserve contact quality. |
| 16 | Lateral Line Hops | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | none, cones | Useful for lateral reactivity and cutting preparation without immediately jumping into high-amplitude bounds. |

### Jump / Projection Power

| # | Exercise | Subrole | Equipment | Why it belongs |
|---:|---|---|---|---|
| 17 | Squat Jump | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | none | The bodyweight jump version of a squat trains force expression quickly instead of load tolerance. |
| 18 | Countermovement Jump | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | none | Classic lower-body power expression that uses the stretch-shortening cycle without external load. |
| 19 | Broad Jump to Stick | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | none, cones | Directly supports first-step acceleration, long jump takeoff preparation, and football line-drive projection. |
| 20 | Triple Broad Jump | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | none, cones | Challenges athletes to re-accelerate through contacts, bridging a single broad jump to sprint and jump sequences. |
| 21 | Tuck Jump | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | none | Trains vertical impulse and quick body repositioning, useful for athletes who need pop and aerial body control. |
| 22 | Split-Squat Jump | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | none | Converts split squat strength into high-speed force expression without using dumbbells, barbells, or kettlebells. |
| 23 | Lunge Switch Jump | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | none | Builds elastic leg switching and fast hip/knee repositioning for sprinting, jumping, and change-of-direction sports. |
| 24 | Sprinter Step-Up Jump | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | box | Links step-up strength to sprint-like hip extension and knee drive while limiting floor takeoff complexity. |
| 25 | Seated Box Jump | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | box | Reduces countermovement reliance and teaches an athlete to produce force from a static start. |
| 26 | Depth Jump to Vertical Jump | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | box | Advanced reactive drill for athletes who already own landing mechanics and need rapid rebound power. |

### Multidirectional / COD / Rotational Projection

| # | Exercise | Subrole | Equipment | Why it belongs |
|---:|---|---|---|---|
| 27 | Lateral Bound to Stick | Deceleration / COD Power | none, cones | Builds the lateral force and braking skill needed for cutting, defending, base stealing, and field-sport battles. |
| 28 | Skater Bound Continuous | Elastic Stiffness Plyometric Rudiments | none, cones | Progresses from single lateral sticks to elastic lateral re-acceleration across contacts. |
| 29 | Rotational Bound to Stick | Deceleration / COD Power | none, cones | Useful for baseball swings, throws, cutting, and any athlete who must rotate force through the ground. |
| 30 | 180-Degree Jump to Stick | Deceleration / COD Power | none | Trains athletes to create and stop rotation quickly rather than spin without control. |
| 31 | Crossover Bound | Deceleration / COD Power | cones | Important for defensive shuffles, base stealing, route releases, and lateral acceleration from staggered positions. |
| 32 | Curved Sprint Bound | Acceleration Start Speed | cones | Develops inside-edge force, body lean, and repeated projection for field-sport curves and approach runs. |
| 33 | Deceleration Re-Acceleration Sprint | Deceleration / COD Power | cones | Trains the exact brake-to-burst quality used when a lineman redirects, a runner hits a cut, or an athlete exits a stop. |
| 34 | 5-10-5 Explosive Plant Drill | Deceleration / COD Power | cones | Turns the pro-agility shape into a quality power drill instead of a repeated conditioning test. |

### Medicine Ball / Rotational / Upper-Body Power

| # | Exercise | Subrole | Equipment | Why it belongs |
|---:|---|---|---|---|
| 35 | Medicine Ball Chest Pass | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | medicine_ball, wall | Builds fast upper-body power for contact, throwing, punching action, and chest-to-hand force transfer. |
| 36 | Medicine Ball Scoop Toss | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | medicine_ball | Mimics horizontal projection and powerful hip extension with lower landing stress than repeated jumps. |
| 37 | Medicine Ball Overhead Slam | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | medicine_ball | Allows high-intent total-body output while reducing lower-body impact and teaching force transfer through the trunk. |
| 38 | Medicine Ball Rotational Throw | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | medicine_ball, wall | High transfer for baseball swings, throws, tennis strokes, lineman hand strikes, and rotational field-sport actions. |
| 39 | Medicine Ball Shot-Put Throw | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | medicine_ball | Great for asymmetrical power, contact extension, throwing athletes, and rotational-to-linear force transfer. |
| 40 | Medicine Ball Side Toss with Step | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | medicine_ball, wall | Adds approach-like rhythm so athletes learn to turn lower-body drive into bat, stick, or throwing-arm speed. |
| 41 | Kneeling Medicine Ball Chest Pass | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | medicine_ball, wall, mat | Removes leg drive to expose trunk stiffness, shoulder speed, and clean horizontal force transfer. |
| 42 | Drop Catch Medicine Ball Chest Pass | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | medicine_ball, partner, wall | Trains upper-body stiffness and re-output similar to contact, blocking hand strikes, and rapid throw-release actions. |
| 43 | Plyo Push-Up | Jump / Throw Explosive Power | none, mat | Bodyweight alternative to loaded pressing when the goal is fast force expression, not strength volume. |

### Reactive / Partner / Game-Speed Explosiveness

| # | Exercise | Subrole | Equipment | Why it belongs |
|---:|---|---|---|---|
| 44 | Reaction Ball Drop Sprint | Reactive Agility / Tumbling Output | partner, cones | Trains fast recognition and acceleration without turning agility into a memorized footwork pattern. |
| 45 | Mirror First-Step Chase | Reactive Agility / Tumbling Output | partner, cones | Useful for linemen, defenders, and court athletes who must explode based on another body, not a countdown. |
| 46 | Tennis Ball Split-Step Sprint | Reactive Agility / Tumbling Output | partner, cones | Combines elastic readiness with visual choice, valuable for hitters, infielders, racket sports, and defensive reactions. |
| 47 | Partner Bump-and-Go Start | Reactive Agility / Tumbling Output | partner, cones | Supports football line play and contact sports by teaching athletes to stay braced and burst after external pressure. |
| 48 | Tag-and-Go Acceleration | Reactive Agility / Tumbling Output | partner, cones | Maintains high intent and decision speed for youth or teams while keeping reps short enough to avoid conditioning creep. |
| 49 | Reactive Lateral Bound Callout | Reactive Agility / Tumbling Output | partner, cones | Blends lateral projection with a real-time decision so athletes cannot pre-plan the bound direction. |
| 50 | Auditory Start Sprint | Reactive Agility / Tumbling Output | partner, cones | Useful for track starts, football cadence, and any athlete who must react explosively to an auditory cue. |
